### [216] [Structural Anchors and Reasoning Fragility:Understanding CoT Robustness in LLM4Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12214)
*Yang Liu,Da Song,Armstrong Foundjem,Heng Li,Foutse Khomh*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: CoT提示在代码生成中的稳健性研究：发现CoT并非总是有益，其效果取决于扰动是否影响推理轨迹中的结构敏感锚点，并识别了三种轨迹变形模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管CoT提示被广泛用于引导大语言模型进行代码生成的显式推理，但其在真实输入扰动下的稳健性和推理轨迹稳定性仍不清楚。先前研究主要通过最终正确性评估CoT，缺乏对其内部不确定性动态如何重塑以及为何有时反而损害代码生成的理解。

Method: 对6个模型和2个代码基准（MHPP和BigCodeBench）进行大规模实证研究，对任务文档字符串施加系统性的字符级、词级和句子级扰动。通过标记级不确定性记录完整生成轨迹，并定义三个新的结构锚点：推理-代码转换、符号承诺和算法表达。

Result: 1) CoT不产生统一的性能或稳健性增益：其益处取决于模型家族、任务结构和提示明确性；2) CoT和No-CoT展现出不同的稳健性特征，不同扰动家族触发不同的失败模式；3) 识别出三种重复出现的轨迹变形——延长、分支和简化，这些变形在扰动与结构锚点交互时系统性地出现；4) 早期不确定性可作为可靠诊断信号，用于定位轨迹不稳定性在敏感锚点周围开始的位置。

Conclusion: CoT的混合性能可通过扰动与结构敏感锚点的交互得到统一解释，这些发现为构建更稳健的基于推理的代码生成器提供了设计原则。

Abstract: Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting is widely used to elicit explicit reasoning from large language models for code (LLM4Code). However, its impact on robustness and the stability of reasoning trajectories under realistic input perturbations remains poorly understood. Prior work has largely evaluated CoT through final correctness, leaving a critical gap in understanding how CoT reshapes internal uncertainty dynamics and why it sometimes harms rather than helps code generation. We suggest that CoT is not uniformly beneficial; instead, its robustness depends on whether perturbations destabilize structurally sensitive commitment points along the reasoning-to-code trajectory. We conduct a controlled, large-scale empirical study of CoT across six models and two code benchmarks (MHPP and BigCodeBench), subjecting task docstrings to systematic character-, word-, and sentence-level perturbations. We instrument full generation traces with token-level uncertainty and define three novel structural anchors: reasoning-code transition, symbolic commitment, and algorithmic articulation. Findings: (1) CoT does not yield uniform performance or robustness gains: its benefits are contingent on model family, task structure, and prompt explicitness. (2) CoT and No-CoT exhibit distinct robustness profiles, with different perturbation families triggering different failure modes. (3) We identify three recurrent trajectory deformations--Lengthening, Branching, and Simplification--that systematically emerge when perturbations interact with structural anchors and explain failure patterns. (4) Early-stage uncertainty serves as a reliable diagnostic signal for localizing where trajectory instability begins around sensitive anchors. These results provide a unified explanation for CoT's mixed performance and suggest design principles for building more robust reasoning-based code generators.

</details>


### [217] [Learning Project-wise Subsequent Code Edits via Interleaving Neural-based Induction and Tool-based Deduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12220)
*Chenyan Liu,Yun Lin,Yuhuan Huang,Jiaxin Chang,Binhang Qi,Bo Jiang,Zhiyong Huang,Jin Song Dong*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: TRACE是一个工具集成的代码编辑推荐系统，通过神经推理和工具推导的交替使用，在项目级代码编辑中平衡预测范围、准确性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM-based的代码编辑解决方案在预测范围、准确性和效率之间存在平衡问题。例如Cursor在局部编辑范围准确率高但跨文件编辑性能下降，CoEdPilot在项目级编辑中存在效率限制。需要一种能同时兼顾范围、准确性和效率的解决方案。

Method: TRACE通过交替使用神经推理（用于语义编辑预测）和工具推导（用于语法编辑预测）来预测后续代码编辑。使用IDE工具（如重构工具、linting工具）进行语法编辑推导，并学习神经模型来决定何时调用IDE工具。同时提出细粒度的编辑表示来提升神经编辑模型的性能。

Result: 论文未提供具体实验结果，但从方法描述来看，TRACE旨在提升项目级代码编辑的预测范围、准确性和效率的平衡。

Conclusion: TRACE是一个创新的代码编辑解决方案，通过结合神经推理和工具推导的方法，解决了现有LLM-based代码编辑工具在范围、准确性和效率之间的平衡问题。

Abstract: In industrial and open-source software engineering tasks, developers often perform project-wise code editing tasks, including feature enhancement, refactoring, and bug fixing, where the leading AI models are expected to support the productivity. Hence, researchers and practitioners have proposed and adopted many LLM-based solutions to facilitate their real-world development. However, they largely suffer from the balance among predicting scope, accuracy, and efficiency. For example, solutions like Cursor achieve high accuracy only in a local editing scope while its performance drops on cross-file edits. In contrast, solutions like CoEdPilot exhibit efficiency limitations when used to predict project-wise edits.
  In this work, we propose TRACE (Tool-integrated RecommendAtion for Code Editing), a novel subsequent code editing solution to push the boundary of scope, accuracy, and efficiency. Our rationale lies in that code edits are triggered for either semantic or syntactic reasons. Therefore, TRACE predicts subsequent edits by interleaving neural-based induction for semantic edit prediction and tool-based deduction for syntactic edit prediction. The tools can be any IDE facilities, such as refactoring tools (e.g., rename) or linting tools (e.g., use-def), providing decent performance of deducing edit-location and edit-generation. Technically, we address the challenge of (1) when to interleave between neural-based and tool-based prediction and (2) how to further improve the performance of neural-based prediction. As for the former, we learn a neural model to detect when to invoke IDE editing tools. As for the latter, we propose a novel and fine-grained editing representation to further boost the performance of neural editing models. ......

### [218] [CodeSpecBench: Benchmarking LLMs for Executable Behavioral Specification Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12268)
*Zaoyu Chen,Jianbo Dai,Boyu Zhu,Jingdong Wang,Huiming Wang,Xin Xu,Haoyang Yuan,Zhijiang Guo,Xiao-Ming Wu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: CodeSpecBench是一个用于评估LLM生成可执行行为规范的基准测试，支持函数级和仓库级任务，发现LLM在仓库级任务上性能显著下降，且规范生成比代码生成更具挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于规范生成的研究在评估方法、任务设置和规范表达能力方面存在局限性，需要更全面的基准来评估LLM对程序行为意图的理解程度。

Method: 构建CodeSpecBench基准，从多样化真实代码库中提取任务，支持函数级和仓库级规范生成，将规范编码为可执行的Python函数，采用基于执行的评估协议。

Result: 评估15个最先进的LLM发现：1）在仓库级任务上性能急剧下降，最佳模型仅达到20.2%通过率；2）规范生成比代码生成更具挑战性；3）强大的编码性能不一定反映对程序语义的深入理解。

Conclusion: CodeSpecBench为评估LLM生成可执行行为规范提供了全面基准，揭示了LLM在理解程序意图方面的局限性，特别是处理复杂仓库级上下文时的困难。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can generate code from natural language, but the extent to which they capture intended program behavior remains unclear. Executable behavioral specifications, defined via preconditions and postconditions, provide a concrete means to assess such understanding. However, existing work on specification generation is constrained in evaluation methodology, task settings, and specification expressiveness. We introduce CodeSpecBench, a benchmark for executable behavioral specification generation under an execution-based evaluation protocol. CodeSpecBench supports both function-level and repository-level tasks and encodes specifications as executable Python functions. Constructed from diverse real-world codebases, it enables a realistic assessment of both correctness (accepting valid behaviors) and completeness (rejecting invalid behaviors). Evaluating 15 state-of-the-art LLMs on CodeSpecBench, we observe a sharp performance degradation on repository-level tasks, where the best model attains only a 20.2% pass rate. We further find that specification generation is substantially more challenging than code generation, indicating that strong coding performance does not necessarily reflect deep understanding of intended program semantics. Our data and code are available at https://github.com/SparksofAGI/CodeSpecBench.

### [219] [LLMs Are Not a Silver Bullet: A Case Study on Software Fairness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12640)
*Xinyue Li,Sixuan Li,Ying Xiao,Jie M. Zhang,Zhou Yang,Xuanzhe Liu,Zhenpeng Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: LLM-based bias mitigation methods在公平性和预测性能上均不如传统ML方法，现有LLM研究的正面结果主要源于人工平衡的测试数据而非真实不平衡分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型(LLMs)的兴起，研究者开始探索其在偏见缓解中的应用，但尚不清楚LLM方法是否优于传统ML方法，软件工程师缺乏实际采用的明确指导。

Method: 进行大规模研究，比较最先进的ML和LLM偏见缓解方法；分析先前LLM研究的评估设置；探索在完整训练集上的监督微调。

Result: ML方法在公平性和预测性能上始终优于LLM方法，即使强大的LLM也无法超越已建立的ML基线；现有LLM研究的优势主要来自人工平衡的测试数据；监督微调虽然能获得有竞争力的结果，但相对于传统ML方法的优势有限。

Conclusion: LLMs并非软件公平性的万能解决方案，传统ML方法在偏见缓解任务上仍然更具优势。

Abstract: Fairness is a critical requirement for human-related, high-stakes software systems, motivating extensive research on bias mitigation. Prior work has largely focused on tabular data settings using traditional Machine Learning (ML) methods. With the rapid rise of Large Language Models (LLMs), recent studies have begun to explore their use for bias mitigation in the same setting. However, it remains unclear whether LLM-based methods offer advantages over traditional ML methods, leaving software engineers without clear guidance for practical adoption. To address this gap, we present a large-scale study comparing state-of-the-art ML- and LLM-based bias mitigation methods. We find that ML-based methods consistently outperform LLM-based methods in both fairness and predictive performance, with even strong LLMs failing to surpass established ML baselines. To understand why prior LLM-based studies report favorable results, we analyze their evaluation settings and show that these gains are largely driven by artificially balanced test data rather than realistic imbalanced distributions. We further observe that existing LLM-based methods primarily rely on in-context learning and thus fail to leverage all available training data. Motivated by this, we explore supervised fine-tuning on the full training set and find that, while it achieves competitive results, its advantages over traditional ML methods remain limited. These findings suggest that LLMs are not a silver bullet for software fairness.

</details>


### [220] [Pricing-Driven Resource Allocation in the Computing Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12642)
*Alejandro García-Fernández,Boris Sedlak,José Antonio Parejo,Pantelis Frangoudis,Antonio Ruiz-Cortés,Schahram Dustdar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文提出使用定价结构作为表示计算连续体中资源配置空间的通用方法，以解决基础设施节点选择的组合优化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在计算连续体中部署应用需要从地理分布和异构环境中选择基础设施节点，同时满足性能、位置等约束。随着基础设施规模和异构性增长，决策空间变得组合爆炸，现有方法使用特定基础设施拓扑和需求表示，难以实现解决方案的泛化。

Method: 1) 提出基于定价的资源分配问题表述，使基础设施配置空间能用定价结构表示；2) 利用PRIME定价分析引擎探索这些空间并计算满足功能和非功能约束的成本最优部署；3) 开发合成基础设施拓扑和工作负载需求的生成过程；4) 创建包含9600个预计算资源分配场景的数据集用于基准测试。

Result: 论文提出了一个完整的框架，将资源配置问题转化为定价表示问题，并提供了相应的工具链和数据集，为计算连续体中的资源分配提供了新的通用解决方案。

Conclusion: 定价结构可以作为表示配置空间的通用方法，为解决计算连续体中的资源配置等配置问题提供了有前景的替代方案，通过将SaaS生态系统的定价概念应用于基础设施配置，实现了更好的泛化能力。

Abstract: Deploying applications across the computing continuum requires selecting infrastructure nodes from geographically distributed and heterogeneous environments while satisfying constraints (e.g., performance, location). This decision problem is an important facet of resource allocation. As infrastructures grow in scale and heterogeneity, the resulting decision space becomes inherently combinatorial. Existing approaches typically formulate this problem as a constrained optimization task using ad-hoc representations of infrastructure topologies and demand, which hinders generalization across solutions. In contrast, Software as a Service ecosystems address a structurally similar configuration problem through pricings -structures whose plans and add-ons implicitly define the configuration space of possible subscriptions. Building on this observation, this work explores the potential of pricings as general-purpose representations of configuration spaces, positioning them as a promising alternative for addressing configuration problems, such as resource allocation, across the computing continuum. To this end, the paper presents the following contributions: i) a pricing-based formulation of the resource allocation problem in the computing continuum, enabling infrastructure configuration spaces to be represented using pricings; ii) a workflow that leverages PRIME, a pricing analysis engine, to explore these spaces and compute cost-optimal deployments satisfying functional and non-functional constraints; iii) generation processes for synthetic infrastructure topologies and workload demands; and iv) a dataset comprising 9,600 precomputed resource allocation scenarios to support benchmarking.

### [221] [Short Version of VERIFAI2026 Paper -- Learning Infused Formal Reasoning: Contract Synthesis, Artefact Reuse and Semantic Foundations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12747)
*Arshad Beg,Diarmuid O'Donoghue,Rosemary Monahan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: LIFR框架整合机器学习与形式验证，通过自动合约合成、验证工件语义复用和数学基础理论，将验证转变为知识驱动的累积过程


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI系统在自然语言处理、感知和决策任务中表现出色，但其行为往往不透明且难以验证，限制了在安全关键系统中的适用性。形式方法虽然提供数学严谨的验证机制，但形式规范的创建和维护劳动密集且难以扩展。

Method: 提出学习注入形式推理（LIFR）研究愿景，整合机器学习技术与形式验证工作流，包括三个研究方向：1）从自然语言需求自动合成合约；2）使用图匹配和学习嵌入实现验证工件的语义复用；3）基于统一编程理论和机构理论的数学基础语义基础。

Result: LIFR框架旨在将验证从孤立的正确性证明转变为累积的知识驱动过程，使规范、合约和证明能够在系统间合成、对齐和复用。

Conclusion: 通过整合机器学习与形式验证，LIFR框架有望解决形式规范创建和维护的扩展性问题，提高AI系统在安全关键应用中的可验证性和可信度。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence systems have achieved remarkable capability in natural language processing, perception and decision-making tasks. However, their behaviour often remains opaque and difficult to verify, limiting their applicability in safety-critical systems. Formal methods provide mathematically rigorous mechanisms for specifying and verifying system behaviour, yet the creation and maintenance of formal specifications remains labour intensive and difficult to scale. This paper outlines a research vision called Learning-Infused Formal Reasoning (LIFR), which integrates machine learning techniques with formal verification workflows. The framework focuses on three complementary research directions: automated contract synthesis from natural language requirements, semantic reuse of verification artifacts using graph matching and learning-based embeddings, and mathematically grounded semantic foundations based on the Unifying Theories of Programming (UTP) and the Theory of Institutions. Together these research threads aim to transform verification from isolated correctness proofs into a cumulative knowledge-driven process where specifications, contracts and proofs can be synthesised, aligned and reused across systems.

These simplifications limit their ability to measure practical generalizability. We present R2Eval1, a benchmark of 135 code reasoning problems drawn from ten widely used Python projects.
